{
  "content": "# Solution: Refactor Event Handling into Shared Event Dispatcher Module\n\n## Overview\n\nThis solution implements a major architectural refactoring by creating a centralized, generic event dispatcher module in the `shared` library. This new module encapsulates the Kafka consumption loop and event routing logic that was previously duplicated across multiple services (`governance_hall`, `mint_factory`, and `muse_observer`).\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Current State (Before Refactoring)\n\nThe three services all implement similar patterns:\n1. **governance_hall/src/event_handler.c** (481 lines): Uses a linked-list of callbacks registered via `event_handler_register()`. The `consumer_loop()` function polls Kafka, parses JSON, validates signatures, and dispatches to registered callbacks by iterating through the linked list.\n\n2. **mint_factory/src/event_handler.c** (431 lines): Uses an enum-based switch statement in `dispatch_event()` to route events. Contains `evh_init()` and `evh_shutdown()` lifecycle functions.\n\n3. **muse_observer/src/event_listener.c** (343 lines): Uses a strategy pattern where a single `MuseActionStrategy` receives all events via `dispatch_event()`.\n\n### Common Patterns Identified\n\nAll three services share:\n- Kafka consumer setup (rd_kafka_conf_set, rd_kafka_new, rd_kafka_subscribe)\n- Main consumption loop with polling\n- JSON parsing with jansson\n- Event type extraction from JSON\n- Handler/callback invocation\n- Graceful shutdown via signal handling\n- Error logging and metrics\n\n### Design Decisions\n\n1. **Hash Map for Handler Registry**: More efficient than linked-list for lookup, especially as the number of handlers grows. Uses open addressing with linear probing for simplicity.\n\n2. **String-based Event Type Keys**: Matches the JSON `\"type\"` field directly, avoiding enum conversion overhead.\n\n3. **Callback Signature**: Uses `(const char* event_type, const char* payload, size_t len, void* user_context)` to support both JSON and potential protobuf payloads.\n\n4. **Thread Safety**: Uses mutex protection for handler registration while the dispatcher is running.\n\n5. **Wildcard Handlers**: Support for handlers that receive all events (like the muse_observer pattern).\n\n---\n\n## New Files to Create\n\n### File 1: `shared/event_dispatcher/hc_event_dispatcher.h`\n\n```c\n/**\n * hc_event_dispatcher.h\n *\n * HoloCanvas - Generic Event Dispatcher Module\n * --------------------------------------------\n * A reusable, generic event dispatcher that centralizes the Kafka consumption\n * loop and event routing logic. This module allows microservices to register\n * handlers for specific event types, abstracting away the boilerplate of\n * Kafka consumer setup, JSON parsing, and event dispatching.\n *\n * Usage:\n *   1. Create a dispatcher with event_dispatcher_create()\n *   2. Register handlers for event types with event_dispatcher_register_handler()\n *   3. */\n/*===========================================================================*/\n\n/**\n * Event handler function signature.\n *\n * Handlers receive:\n *   - event_type: The string key during dispatcher creation\n *\n * Returns:\n *   HC_OK on success, or an appropriate error code on failure.\n */\ntypedef hc_error_t (*event_handler_func_t)(const char *event_type,\n                                           const char *payload,\n                                           size_t payload_len,\n                                           void *user_context);\n\n/**\n * Alternative handler signature that receives parsed protobuf message.\n * Only used if protobuf-c is available.\n */\ntypedef hc_error_t (*event_handler_proto_func_t)(const ProtobufCMessage *msg,\n                                                  void *user_context);\n\n/**\n * Opaque event dispatcher context.\n */\ntypedef struct EventDispatcher EventDispatcher;\n\n/**\n * Configuration for the event dispatcher.\n */\ntypedef struct {\n    const char *kafka_brokers;   /**< Comma-separated list of Kafka brokers */\n    const char *topic;           /**< Topic to subscribe to */\n    const char *group_id;        /**< Consumer group ID */\n    int poll_timeout_ms;         /**< Kafka poll timeout (default: 500ms) */\n    int max_handlers;            /**< Maximum number of handlers (default: 64) */\n} EventDispatcherConfig;\n\n/*===========================================================================*/\n/* Public API                                                                */\n/*===========================================================================*/\n\n/**\n * Create a new event dispatcher.\n *\n * @param kafka_brokers Comma-separated list of Kafka broker config       Configuration structure\n * @param user_context User-provided context passed to all handlers\n *\n * @return A new EventDispatcher instance, or NULL on failure\n */\nEventDispatcher *event_dispatcher_create_ex(const EventDispatcherConfig *config,\n                                            void *user_context);\n\n/**\n * Register an event handler for a specific event type.\n *\n * The event_type_key is matched against the \"type\" field in incoming JSON\n * messages. Multiple handlers can be registered for the same event type;\n * they will be called in registration order.\n *\n * @param dispatcher     The event dispatcher instance\n * @param event_type_key The event type string to match (e.g., \"VOTE_CAST\")\n * @param handler        The handler function to invoke for matching events\n *\n * @return HC_OK on success, error code on failure\n */\nhc_error_t event_dispatcher_register_handler(EventDispatcher *dispatcher,\n                                             const char *event_type_key,\n                                             event_handler_func_t handler);\n\n/**\n * Register a wildcard handler that receives all events.\n *\n * Wildcard handlers are called after type-specific handlers.\n *\n * @param dispatcher The event dispatcher instance\n * @param handler    The handler function to invoke for all events\n *\n * @return HC_OK on success, error code on failure\n */\nhc_error_t event_dispatcher_register_wildcard(EventDispatcher *dispatcher,\n                                              event_handler_func_t handler);\n\n/**\n * Start the event consumption and dispatch loop.\n *\n * This function blocks and continuously polls Kafka for messages, dispatching\n * them to registered handlers. @param dispatcher The event dispatcher instance\n */\nvoid event_dispatcher_run(EventDispatcher *dispatcher);\n\n/**\n * Signal the dispatcher to stop processing events.\n *\n * This is thread-safe and can be called from signal handlers.\n *\n * @param dispatcher The event dispatcher instance\n */\nvoid event_dispatcher_stop(EventDispatcher *dispatcher);\n\n/**\n * Check if the dispatcher is currently running.\n *\n * @param dispatcher The event dispatcher instance\n * @return true if running, false otherwise\n */\nbool event_dispatcher_is_running(const EventDispatcher *dispatcher);\n\n/**\n * Destroy the event dispatcher and free all resources.\n *\n * If the dispatcher is still running, this function will stop it first.\n *\n * @param dispatcher The event   uint64_t events_dispatched;\n    uint64_t events_unhandled;\n    uint64_t parse_errors;\n    uint64_t handler_errors;\n} EventDispatcherStats;\n\n/**\n * Get current statistics from the dispatcher.\n *\n * @param dispatcher The event dispatcher instance\n * @param stats      Output parameter for statistics\n *\n * @return HC_OK on success\n */\nhc_error_t event_dispatcher_get_stats(const EventDispatcher *dispatcher,\n                                      EventDispatcherStats *stats);\n\n/*===========================================================================*/\n/* Convenience Macros                                                        */\n/*===========================================================================*/\n\n/**\n * Install signal handlers for graceful shutdown.\n *\n * This macro sets up SIGINT and SIGTERM handlers that call\n * event_dispatcher_stop() on the given dispatcher.\n */\n#define EVENT_DISPATCHER_INSTALL_SIGNALS(dispatcher) \\\n    event_dispatcher_install_signal_handlers(dispatcher)\n\nvoid event_dispatcher_install_signal_handlers(EventDispatcher *dispatcher);\n\n#ifdef __cplusplus\n}\n#endif\n\n#endif /* HOLOCANVAS_SHARED_EVENT_DISPATCHER_H */\n```\n\n### File 2: `shared/event_dispatcher/hc_event_dispatcher.c`\n\n```c\n/**\n * hc_event_dispatcher.c\n *\n * HoloCanvas - Generic Event Dispatcher Implementation\n * -----------------------------------------------------\n * Implementation of the centralized event dispatcher module.\n *\n * Copyright (c) 2023-2024 The HoloCanvas contributors\n * SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0\n */\n\n#define _POSIX_C_SOURCE 200809L\n\n#include \"hc_event_dispatcher.h\"\n\n#include <errno.h>\n#include <pthread.h>\n#include <signal.h>\n#include <stdatomic.h>\n#include <stdio.h>\n#include <stdlib.h>\n#include <string.h>\n#include <time.h>\n\n#include <jansson.h>\n#include <librdkafka/rdkafka.h>\n\n/*===========================================================================*/\n/* Configuration Defaults                                                    */\n/*===========================================================================*/\n\n#define DEFAULT_POLL_TIMEOUT_MS  500\n#define DEFAULT_MAX_HANDLERS     64\n#define HANDLER_MAP_LOAD_FACTOR  0.75\n#define MAX_EVENT_TYPE_LEN       128\n\n/*===========================================================================*/\n/* Logging                                                                   */\n/*===========================================================================*/\n\n#define LOG_PREFIX \"[EventDispatcher] \"\n#define LOG_ERROR(fmt, ...) fprintf(stderr, LOG_PREFIX \"ERROR: \" fmt \"\\n\", ##__VA_ARGS__)\n#define LOG_WARN(fmt, ...)  fprintf(stderr, LOG_PREFIX \"WARN:  \" fmt \"\\n\", ##__VA_ARGS__)\n#define LOG_INFO(fmt, ...)  fprintf(stdout, LOG_PREFIX \"INFO:  \" fmt \"\\n\", ##__VA_ARGS__)\n#define LOG_DEBUG(fmt, ...) fprintf(stdout, LOG_PREFIX \"DEBUG: \" fmt \"\\n\", ##__VA_ARGS__)\n\n/*===========================================================================*/\n/* Internal Data Structures                                                  */\n/*===========================================================================*/\n\n/**\n * Hash map entry for event handlers.\n * Uses open addressing with linear probing.\n */\ntypedef struct {\n    char *event_type;               /**< Event type key (owned) */\n    event_handler_func_t handler;   /**< Handler function */\n    bool occupied;                  /**< Slot occupied flag */\n} HandlerEntry;\n\n/**\n * Linked list node for multiple handlers on same event type.\n */\ntypedef struct HandlerNode {\n    event_handler_func_t handler;\n    struct HandlerNode *next;\n} HandlerNode;\n\n/**\n * Hash map bucket with chaining for collision handling.\n */\ntypedef struct {\n    char *event_type;       /**< Event type key (owned) */\n    HandlerNode *handlers;  /**< Linked list of handlers */\n} HandlerBucket;\n\n/**\n * Internal dispatcher state.\n */\nstruct EventDispatcher {\n    /* Kafka handles */\n    rd_kafka_t *rk;\n    rd_kafka_conf_t *rk_conf;\n    rd_kafka_topic_partition_list_t *sub_topics;\n\n    /* Configuration */\n    char *kafka_brokers;\n    char *topic;\n    char *group_id;\n    int poll_timeout_ms;\n\n    /* Handler registry (hash map with chaining) */\n    HandlerBucket *handler_map;\n    size_t handler_map_size;\n    size_t handler_count;\n\n    /* Wildcard handlers */\n    HandlerNode *wildcard_handlers;\n\n    /* Thread safety */\n    pthread_mutex_t handler_lock;\n\n    /* Runtime state */\n    atomic_bool running;\n    void *user_context;\n\n    /* Statistics */\n    atomic_uint_fast64_t stats_received;\n    atomic_uint_fast64_t stats_dispatched;\n    atomic_uint_fast64_t stats_unhandled;\n    atomic_uint_fast64_t stats_parse_errors;\n    atomic_uint_fast64_t stats_handler_errors;\n};\n\n/* Global dispatcher for signal handling */\nstatic EventDispatcher *g_signal_dispatcher = NULL;\n\n/*===========================================================================*/\n/* Hash Function                                                             */\n/*===========================================================================*/\n\n/**\n * djb2 hash function for strings.\n */\nstatic size_t hash_string(const char *str) {\n    size_t hash = 5381;\n    int c;\n    while ((c = *str++)) {\n        hash = ((hash << 5) + hash) + (size_t)c;\n    }\n    return hash;\n}\n\n/*===========================================================================*/\n/* Handler Map Operations                                                    */\n/*===========================================================================*/\n\nstatic HandlerBucket *handler_map_find(EventDispatcher *self, const char *event_type) {\n    if (!self->handler_map || !event_type) return NULL;\n\n    size_t idx = hash_string(event_type) % self->handler_map_size;\n\n    /* Linear probing */\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < self->handler_map_size; ++i) {\n        size_t probe_idx = (idx + i) % self->handler_map_size;\n        HandlerBucket *bucket = &self->handler_map[probe_idx];\n\n        if (!bucket->event_type) {\n            return NULL; /* Empty slot - not found */\n        }\n\n        if (strcmp(bucket->event_type, event_type) == 0) {\n            return bucket;\n        }\n    }\n\n    return NULL;\n}\n\nstatic hc_error_t handler_map_insert(EventDispatcher *self,\n                                     const char *event_type,\n                                     event_handler_func_t handler) {\n    if (!self->handler_map || !event_type || !handler) {\n        return HC_ERROR_PACK(HC_SUBSYS_COMMON, HC_SEV_ERROR, HC_EC_INVALID_ARGUMENT);\n    }\n\n    /* Check load factor */\n    if ((double)self->handler_count / (double)self->handler_map_size > HANDLER_MAP_LOAD_FACTOR) {\n        LOG_WARN(\"Handler map approaching capacity limit\");\n    }\n\n    /* Find or create bucket */\n    size_t idx = hash_string(event_type) % self->handler_map_size;\n    HandlerBucket *bucket = NULL;\n\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < self->handler_map_size; ++i) {\n        size_t probe_idx = (idx + i) % self->handler_map_size;\n        HandlerBucket *probe = &self->handler_map[probe_idx];\n\n        if (!probe->event_type) {\n            /* Empty slot - use it */\n            probe->event_type = strdup(event_type);\n            if (!probe->event_type) {\n                return HC_ERROR_PACK(HC_SUBSYS_COMMON, HC_SEV_ERROR, HC_EC_OUT_OF_MEMORY);\n            }\n            probe->handlers = NULL;\n            bucket = probe;\n            self->handler_count++;\n            break;\n        }\n\n        if (strcmp(probe->event_type, event_type) == 0) {\n            /* Existing bucket for this event type */\n            bucket = probe;\n            break;\n        }\n    }\n\n    if (!bucket) {\n        LOG_ERROR(\"Handler map is full\");\n        return HC_ERROR_PACK(HC_SUBSYS_COMMON, HC_SEV_ERROR, HC_EC_OUT_OF_MEMORY);\n    }\n\n    /* Add handler to bucket's linked list */\n    HandlerNode *node = malloc(sizeof(HandlerNode));\n    if (!node) {\n        return HC_ERROR_PACK(HC_SUBSYS_COMMON, HC_SEV_ERROR, HC_EC_OUT_OF_MEMORY);\n    }\n\n    node->handler = handler;\n    node->next = bucket->handlers;\n    bucket->handlers = node;\n\n    return HC_OK;\n}\n\nstatic void handler_map_destroy(EventDispatcher *self) {\n    if (!self->handler_map) return;\n\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < self->handler_map_size; ++i) {\n        HandlerBucket *bucket = &self->handler_map[i];\n\n        if (bucket->event_type) {\n            free(bucket->event_type);\n\n            /* Free handler nodes */\n            HandlerNode *node = bucket->handlers;\n            while (node) {\n                HandlerNode *next = node->next;\n                free(node);\n                node = next;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    free(self->handler_map);\n    self->handler_map = NULL;\n}\n\n/*===========================================================================*/\n/* Event Processing                                                          */\n/*===========================================================================*/\n\nstatic int dispatch_to_handlers(EventDispatcher *self,\n                                const char *event_type,\n                                const char *payload,\n                                size_t payload_len) {\n    int handlers_called = 0;\n    bool had_errors = false;\n\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&self->handler_lock);\n\n    /* Find handlers for this event type */\n    HandlerBucket *bucket = handler_map_find(self, event_type);\n    if (bucket && bucket->handlers) {\n        for (HandlerNode *node = bucket->handlers; node; node = node->next) {\n            hc_error_t err = node->handler(event_type, payload, payload_len, self->user_context);\n            handlers_called++;\n\n            if (err != HC_OK) {\n                LOG_WARN(\"Handler for '%s' returned error: %s\", event_type, hc_error_str(err));\n                had_errors = true;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /* Call wildcard handlers */\n    for (HandlerNode *node = self->wildcard_handlers; node; node = node->next) {\n        hc_error_t err = node->handler(event_type, payload, payload_len, self->user_context);\n        handlers_called++;\n\n        if (err != HC_OK) {\n            LOG_WARN(\"Wildcard handler returned error: %s\", hc_error_str(err));\n            had_errors = true;\n        }\n    }\n\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&self->handler_lock);\n\n    if (had_errors) {\n        atomic_fetch_add(&self->stats_handler_errors, 1);\n    }\n\n    return handlers_called;\n}\n\nstatic void process_message(EventDispatcher *self,\n                           const void *payload,\n                           size_t len) {\n    atomic_fetch_add(&self->stats_received, 1);\n\n    /* Parse JSON */\n    json_error_t jerr;\n    json_t *root = json_loadb((const char *)payload, len, 0, &jerr);\n    if (!root) {\n        LOG_WARN(\"JSON parse error at line %d: %s\", jerr.line, jerr.text);\n        atomic_fetch_add(&self->stats_parse_errors, 1);\n        return;\n    }\n\n    /* Extract event type */\n    json_t *type_json = json_object_get(root, \"type\");\n    if (!json_is_string(type_json)) {\n        LOG_WARN(\"Event missing 'type' field\");\n        json_decref(root);\n        atomic_fetch_add(&self->stats_parse_errors, 1);\n        return;\n    }\n\n    const char *event_type = json_string_value(type_json);\n\n    /* Extract payload (or use entire message) */\n    json_t *payload_json = json_object_get(root, \"payload\");\n    char *payload_str = NULL;\n    size_t payload_len = 0;\n\n    if (payload_json) {\n        payload_str = json_dumps(payload_json, JSON_COMPACT);\n        payload_len = payload_str ? strlen(payload_str) : 0;\n    } else {\n        /* Use entire message as payload */\n        payload_str = strndup((const char *)payload, len);\n        payload_len = len;\n    }\n\n    if (!payload_str) {\n        LOG_ERROR(\"Failed to extract payload\");\n        json_decref(root);\n        return;\n    }\n\n    /* Dispatch to handlers */\n    int handlers_called = dispatch_to_handlers(self, event_type, payload_str, payload_len);\n\n    if (handlers_called > 0) {\n        atomic_fetch_add(&self->stats_dispatched, 1);\n        LOG_DEBUG(\"Event '%s' dispatched to %d handler(s)\", event_type, handlers_called);\n    } else {\n        atomic_fetch_add(&self->stats_unhandled, 1);\n        LOG_DEBUG(\"No handlers for event type '%s'\", event_type);\n    }\n\n    free(payload_str);\n    json_decref(root);\n}\n\n/*===========================================================================*/\n/* Consumer Loop                                                             */\n/*===========================================================================*/\n\nstatic void consumer_loop(EventDispatcher *self) {\n    LOG_INFO(\"Event dispatcher consumer loop started\");\n\n    while (atomic_load(&self->running)) {\n        rd_kafka_message_t *rkmsg = rd_kafka_consumer_poll(self->rk, self->poll_timeout_ms);\n\n        if (!rkmsg) {\n            continue; /* Timeout - poll again */\n        }\n\n        if (rkmsg->err) {\n            if (rkmsg->err == RD_KAFKA_RESP_ERR__PARTITION_EOF) {\n                /* End of partition - not an error */\n                rd_kafka_message_destroy(rkmsg);\n                continue;\n            }\n            LOG_WARN(\"Kafka error: %s\", rd_kafka_message_errstr(rkmsg));\n            rd_kafka_message_destroy(rkmsg);\n            continue;\n        }\n\n        /* Process the message */\n        process_message(self, rkmsg->payload, rkmsg->len);\n\n        rd_kafka_message_destroy(rkmsg);\n    }\n\n    LOG_INFO(\"Event dispatcher consumer loop stopped\");\n}\n\n/*===========================================================================*/\n/* Signal Handling                                                           */\n/*===========================================================================*/\n\nstatic void signal_handler(int sig) {\n    (void)sig;\n    if (g_signal_dispatcher) {\n        event_dispatcher_stop(g_signal_dispatcher);\n    }\n}\n\nvoid event_dispatcher_install_signal_handlers(EventDispatcher *dispatcher) {\n    g_signal_dispatcher = dispatcher;\n\n    struct sigaction sa = {\n        .sa_handler = signal_handler,\n        .sa_flags = 0\n    };\n    sigemptyset(&sa.sa_mask);\n\n    sigaction(SIGINT, &sa, NULL);\n    sigaction(SIGTERM, &sa, NULL);\n}\n\n/*===========================================================================*/\n/* Public API Implementation                                                 */\n/*===========================================================================*/\n\nEventDispatcher *event_dispatcher_create(const char *kafka_brokers,\n                                         const char *topic,\n                                         const char *group_id,\n                                         void *user_context) {\n    EventDispatcherConfig config = {\n        .kafka_brokers = kafka_brokers,\n        .topic = topic,\n        .group_id = group_id,\n        .poll_timeout_ms = DEFAULT_POLL_TIMEOUT_MS,\n        .max_handlers = DEFAULT_MAX_HANDLERS\n    };\n    return event_dispatcher_create_ex(&config, user_context);\n}\n\nEventDispatcher *event_dispatcher_create_ex(const EventDispatcherConfig *config,\n                                            void *user_context) {\n    if (!config || !config->kafka_brokers || !config->topic || !config->group_id) {\n        LOG_ERROR(\"Invalid configuration\");\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    EventDispatcher *self = calloc(1, sizeof(EventDispatcher));\n    if (!self) {\n        LOG_ERROR(\"Out of memory\");\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    /* Store configuration */\n    self->kafka_brokers = strdup(config->kafka_brokers);\n    self->topic = strdup(config->topic);\n    self->group_id = strdup(config->group_id);\n    self->poll_timeout_ms = config->poll_timeout_ms > 0 ? config->poll_timeout_ms : DEFAULT_POLL_TIMEOUT_MS;\n    self->user_context = user_context;\n\n    if (!self->kafka_brokers || !self->topic || !self->group_id) {\n        LOG_ERROR(\"Out of memory for configuration strings\");\n        goto fail;\n    }\n\n    /* Initialize handler map */\n    size_t map_size = (size_t)(config->max_handlers > 0 ? config->max_handlers : DEFAULT_MAX_HANDLERS);\n    self->handler_map_size = map_size * 2; /* Extra space for load factor */\n    self->handler_map = calloc(self->handler_map_size, sizeof(HandlerBucket));\n    if (!self->handler_map) {\n        LOG_ERROR(\"Out of memory for handler map\");\n        goto fail;\n    }\n\n    /* Initialize mutex */\n    if (pthread_mutex_init(&self->handler_lock, NULL) != 0) {\n        LOG_ERROR(\"Failed to initialize mutex\");\n        goto fail;\n    }\n\n    /* Create Kafka configuration */\n    char errstr[512];\n    self->rk_conf = rd_kafka_conf_new();\n\n    if (rd_kafka_conf_set(self->rk_conf, \"bootstrap.servers\",\n                          self->kafka_brokers, errstr, sizeof(errstr)) != RD_KAFKA_CONF_OK) {\n        LOG_ERROR(\"Kafka conf error: %s\", errstr);\n        goto fail;\n    }\n\n    if (rd_kafka_conf_set(self->rk_conf, \"group.id\",\n                          self->group_id, errstr, sizeof(errstr)) != RD_KAFKA_CONF_OK) {\n        LOG_ERROR(\"Kafka conf error: %s\", errstr);\n        goto fail;\n    }\n\n    /* Enable auto-commit for simplicity */\n    rd_kafka_conf_set(self->rk_conf, \"enable.auto.commit\", \"true\", NULL, 0);\n    rd_kafka_conf_set(self->rk_conf, \"auto.offset.reset\", \"earliest\", NULL, 0);\n\n    /* Create consumer */\n    self->rk = rd_kafka_new(RD_KAFKA_CONSUMER, self->rk_conf,\n                            errstr, sizeof(errstr));\n    if (!self->rk) {\n        LOG_ERROR(\"Failed to create Kafka consumer: %s\", errstr);\n        goto fail;\n    }\n\n    rd_kafka_poll_set_consumer(self->rk);\n\n    /* Subscribe to topic */\n    self->sub_topics = rd_kafka_topic_partition_list_new(1);\n    rd_kafka_topic_partition_list_add(self->sub_topics, self->topic, RD_KAFKA_PARTITION_UA);\n\n    if (rd_kafka_subscribe(self->rk, self->sub_topics) != RD_KAFKA_RESP_ERR_NO_ERROR) {\n        LOG_ERROR(\"Failed to subscribe to topic '%s'\", self->topic);\n        goto fail;\n    }\n\n    atomic_init(&self->running, false);\n    atomic_init(&self->stats_received, 0);\n    atomic_init(&self->stats_dispatched, 0);\n    atomic_init(&self->stats_unhandled, 0);\n self->kafka_brokers, self->topic, self->group_id);\n\n    return self;\n\nfail:\n    event_dispatcher_destroy(self);\n    return NULL;\n}\n\nhc_error_t event_dispatcher_register_handler(EventDispatcher *dispatcher,\n                                             const char *event_type_key,\n                                             event_handler_func_t handler) {\n    if (!dispatcher || !event_type_key || !handler) {\n        return HC_ERROR_PACK(HC_SUBSYS_COMMON, HC_SEV_ERROR, HC_EC_INVALID_ARGUMENT);\n    }\n\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&dispatcher->handler_lock);\n    hc_error_t err = handler_map_insert(dispatcher, event_type_key, handler);\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&dispatcher->handler_lock);\n\n    if (err == HC_OK) {\n        LOG_INFO(\"Registered handler for event type '%s'\", event_type_key);\n    }\n\n    return err;\n}\n\nhc_error_t event_dispatcher_register_wildcard(EventDispatcher *dispatcher,\n                                              event_handler_func_t handler) {\n    if (!dispatcher || !handler) {\n        return HC_ERROR_PACK(HC_SUBSYS_COMMON, HC_SEV_ERROR, HC_EC_INVALID_ARGUMENT);\n    }\n\n    HandlerNode *node = malloc(sizeof(HandlerNode));\n    if (!node) {\n        return HC_ERROR_PACK(HC_SUBSYS_COMMON, HC_SEV_ERROR, HC_EC_OUT_OF_MEMORY);\n    }\n\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&dispatcher->handler_lock);\n    node->handler = handler;\n    node->next = dispatcher->wildcard_handlers;\n    dispatcher->wildcard_handlers = node;\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&dispatcher->handler_lock);\n\n    LOG_INFO(\"Registered wildcard handler\");\n    return HC_OK;\n}\n\nvoid event_dispatcher_run(EventDispatcher *dispatcher) {\n    if (!dispatcher) return;\n\n    if (atomic_exchange(&dispatcher->running, true)) {\n        LOG_WARN(\"Dispatcher is already running\");\n        return;\n    }\n\n    consumer_loop(dispatcher);\n}\n\nvoid event_dispatcher_stop(EventDispatcher *dispatcher) {\n    if (!dispatcher) return;\n\n    LOG_INFO(\"Stopping event dispatcher...\");\n    atomic_store(&dispatcher->running, false);\n}\n\nbool event_dispatcher_is_running(const EventDispatcher *dispatcher) {\n    if (!dispatcher) return false;\n    return atomic_load(&dispatcher->running);\n}\n\nvoid event_dispatcher_destroy(EventDispatcher *dispatcher) {\n    if (!dispatcher) return;\n\n    /* Stop if running */\n    if (atomic_load(&dispatcher->running)) {\n        event_dispatcher_stop(dispatcher);\n    }\n\n    /* Clean up Kafka resources */\n    if (dispatcher->rk) {\n        rd_kafka_consumer_close(dispatcher->rk);\n        rd_kafka_destroy(dispatcher->rk);\n    }\n\n    if (dispatcher->sub_topics) {\n        rd_kafka_topic_partition_list_destroy(dispatcher->sub_topics);\n    }\n\n    /* Clean up handler map */\n    handler_map_destroy(dispatcher);\n\n    /* Clean up wildcard handlers */\n    HandlerNode *node = dispatcher->wildcard_handlers;\n    while (node) {\n        HandlerNode *next = node->next;\n        free(node);\n        node = next;\n    }\n\n    /* Clean up mutex */\n    pthread_mutex_destroy(&dispatcher->handler_lock);\n\n    /* Free configuration strings */\n    free(dispatcher->kafka_brokers);\n    free(dispatcher->topic);\n    free(dispatcher->group_id);\n\n    /* Clear global signal handler reference */\n    if (g_signal_dispatcher == dispatcher) {\n        g_signal_dispatcher = NULL;\n    }\n\n    free(dispatcher);\n\n    LOG_INFO(\"Event dispatcher destroyed\");\n}\n\nhc_error_t event_dispatcher_get_stats(const EventDispatcher *dispatcher,\n                                      EventDispatcherStats *stats) {\n    if (!dispatcher || !stats) {\n        return HC_ERROR_PACK(HC_SUBSYS_COMMON, HC_SEV_ERROR, HC_EC_INVALID_ARGUMENT);\n    }\n\n    stats->events_received = atomic_load(&dispatcher->stats_received);\n    stats->events_dispatched = atomic_load(&dispatcher->stats_dispatched);\n    stats->events_unhandled = atomic_load(&dispatcher->stats_unhandled);\n    stats->parse_errors = atomic_load(&dispatcher->stats_parse_errors);\n    stats->handler_errors = atomic_load(&dispatcher->stats_handler_errors);\n\n    return HC_OK;\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Modifications to Existing Files\n\n### Modification 1: Update Observer Event Handler (Refactored)\n *\n * Single wildcard handler that processes all events through the strategy system.\n */\n\n#include <stdio.h>\n#include <stdlib.h>\n#include ##__VA_ARGS__)\n#define LOG_WARN(fmt, ...)  syslog(LOG_WARNING, \"[muse/handler] \" fmt, ##__VA_ARGS__)\n#define LOG_ERROR(fmt, ...) syslog(LOG_ERR, \"[muse/handler] \" fmt, ##__VA_ARGS__)\n\n/* Forward declaration for context structure */\ntypedef struct {\n    char *plugin_dir;\n    char *grpc_target;\n} MuseContext;\n\n/* Strategy function signature */\ntypedef int (*strategy_fn)(const {0};\n\n/* Stub gRPC call */\nstatic int grpc_send_evolution(const char *grpc_target, const char *recipe_json) {\n    (void)grpc_target;\n    LOG_INFO(\"Stub gRPC call: %s\", recipe_json);\n    return 0;\n}\n\n/* Load strategy plugin */\nstatic int load_strategy(const char *plugin_dir, const char *strategy_name) {\n    if (g_plugin_handle && strcmp(g_current_strategy, strategy_name) == 0) {\n        return 0; /* Already loaded */\n    }\n\n    /* Unload previous */\n    if (g_plugin_handle) {\n        dlclose(g_plugin_handle);\n        g_plugin_handle = NULL;\n        g_strategy_run = NULL;\n    }\n\n    /* Load new */\n    char path[512];\n    snprintf(path, sizeof(path), \"%s/lib%s.so\", plugin_dir, strategy_name);\n\n    g_plugin_handle = dlopen(path, RTLD_NOW | RTLD_LOCAL);\n    if (!g_plugin_handle) {\n        LOG_ERROR(\"dlopen failed for %s: %s\", strategy_name, dlerror());\n        return -1;\n    }\n\n    g_strategy_run = (strategy_fn)dlsym(g_plugin_handle, \"muse_strategy_run\");\n    if (!g_strategy_run) {\n        LOG_ERROR(\"Missing muse_strategy_run in %s\", strategy_name);\n        dlclose(g_plugin_handle);\n        g_plugin_handle = NULL;\n        return -1;\n    }\n\n    strncpy(g_current_strategy, strategy_name, sizeof(g_current_strategy) - 1);\n    LOG_INFO(\"Loaded strategy: %s\", strategy_name);\n    return 0;\n}\n\n/**\n * Wildcard handler for all Muse events.\n */\nhc_error_t handle_muse_event(const char *event_type,\n                             const char *payload,\n                             size_t payload_len,\n                             void *user_context) {\n    (void)payload_len;\n\n    MuseContext *ctx = (MuseContext *)user_context;\n\n    LOG_INFO(\"Received event: %s\", event_type);\n\n    json_error_t jerr;\n    json_t *root = json_loads(payload, 0, &jerr);\n    if (!root) {\n        LOG_WARN(\"Invalid JSON: %s\", jerr.text);\n        return HC_ERROR_PACK(HC_SUBSYS_COMMON, HC_SEV_WARNING, HC_EC_DATA_CORRUPT);\n    }\n\n    /* Check for strategy field */\n    const char *strategy = json_string_value(json_object_get(root, \"strategy\"));\n    if (!strategy) {\n        LOG_INFO(\"No strategy specified; ignoring event\");\n        json_decref(root);\n        return HC_OK;\n    }\n\n    /* Load strategy plugin */\n    if (load_strategy(ctx->plugin_dir, strategy) != 0) {\n        json_decref(root);\n        return HC_ERROR_PACK(HC_SUBSYS_COMMON, HC_SEV_ERROR, HC_EC_DEPENDENCY_FAILURE);\n    }\n\n    /* Execute strategy */\n    char *recipe_json = NULL;\n    int rc = g_strategy_run(payload, &recipe_json);\n    if (rc != 0 || !recipe_json) {\n        LOG_ERROR(\"Strategy '%s' failed (rc=%d)\", strategy, rc);\n        json_decref(root);\n        return HC_ERROR_PACK(HC_SUBSYS_COMMON, HC_SEV_ERROR, HC_EC_DEPENDENCY_FAILURE);\n    }\n\n    /* Send to Mint-Factory */\n    rc = grpc_send_evolution(ctx->grpc_target, recipe_json);\n    free(recipe_json);\n\n    json_decref(root);\n    return rc == 0 ? HC_OK : HC_ERROR_PACK(HC_SUBSYS_COMMON, HC_SEV_ERROR, HC_EC_NETWORK_UNREACHABLE);\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Summary of Changes\n\n### New Files Created\n\n| File | Description |\n|------|-------------|\n| /**
 * hc_event_dispatcher.h
 *
 * HoloCanvas - Generic Event Dispatcher Module
 * --------------------------------------------
 * A reusable, generic event dispatcher that centralizes the Kafka consumption
 * loop and event routing logic. This module allows microservices to register
 * handlers for specific event types, abstracting away the boilerplate of
 * Kafka consumer setup, JSON parsing, and event dispatching.
 *
 * Usage:
 *   1. Create a dispatcher with event_dispatcher_create()
 *   2. Register handlers for event types with event_dispatcher_register_handler()
 *   3. Start the event loop with event_dispatcher_run()
 *   4. Clean up with event_dispatcher_destroy()
 *
 * Copyright (c) 2023-2024 The HoloCanvas contributors
 * SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0
 */

#define HOLOCANVAS_SHARED_EVENT_DISPATCHER_H

# Solution: Refactor Event Handling into Shared Event Dispatcher Module

## Overview

This solution implements a major architectural refactoring by creating a centralized, generic event dispatcher module in the `shared` library. This new module encapsulates the Kafka consumption loop and event routing logic that was previously duplicated across multiple services (`governance_hall`, `mint_factory`, and `muse_observer`).

## Analysis

### Current State (Before Refactoring)

The three services all implement similar patterns:
1. **governance_hall/src/event_handler.c** (481 lines): Uses a linked-list of callbacks registered via `event_handler_register()`. The `consumer_loop()` function polls Kafka, parses JSON, validates signatures, and dispatches to registered callbacks by iterating through the linked list.

2. **mint_factory/src/event_handler.c** (431 lines): Uses an enum-based switch statement in `dispatch_event()` to route events. Contains `evh_init()` and `evh_shutdown()` lifecycle functions.

3. **muse_observer/src/event_listener.c** (343 lines): Uses a strategy pattern where a single `MuseActionStrategy` receives all events via `dispatch_event()`.

### Common Patterns Identified

All three services share:
- Kafka consumer setup (rd_kafka_conf_set, rd_kafka_new, rd_kafka_subscribe)
- Main consumption loop with polling
- JSON parsing with jansson
- Event type extraction from JSON
- Handler/callback invocation
- Graceful shutdown via signal handling
- Error logging and metrics

### Design Decisions

1. **Hash Map for Handler Registry**: More efficient than linked-list for lookup, especially as the number of handlers grows. Uses open addressing with linear probing for simplicity.

2. **String-based Event Type Keys**: Matches the JSON `"type"` field directly, avoiding enum
... (truncated)
